We are from out of state trying a support a black owned business, but in our time here we weren't able to taste the food due to the disorganization. The hours on google were incorrect so we were waiting thinking they opened at a specific time. Then we were able to reach a number and were told that they were closed on Monday's, but open @1230 on Tue-Sat.

We were also informed to check instagram for the hours and days of operation. We saw the hours on instagram for Tuesday stated that they were open until 7. But when we tried to place a call in order about 5ish,  we received a text that they were closed and didn't open until Wednesday @ 1130.

I hope the next time we come to town they are actually open according to their posted hours or update the hours if they decide to close early</review>

< text>
So prices have gone up since my last visit, but I have to admit, I‚Äôm not mad. Who‚Äôs prices haven‚Äôt gone up since Covid? It‚Äôs still a great value and they are definitely less expensive than some other sandwich spots I frequent.

Anyway, don‚Äôt get near Montebello as much as I would like anymore, so when I do, you try to grab a roast beef sando since it‚Äôs pretty unique here. The believe it‚Äôs still made on the store, so you are not getting sliced up deli meat that you can get anywhere. I was also craving a sub, so I got both which was a mistake. Two large sando‚Äôs for less than $18 is a deal, but I ate half the sub on my drive home, so I only had enough room for about a 1/4 of my roast beef :). Happy to have left overs, so all good there, but I definitely will gain weight if I order like I did.

Service is always spot on. This trip was a call ahead order which they said would be ready on 10 mins, but told them  was 20 mins away, so they said they would hold off a bit before making so it would be fresh. How cool was that.

Best straight forward sandwich and prices in the San Gabriel valley for sure. I have a Italian sub option in another city when I need it, but Tony‚Äôs is my only spot for roast beef!!!!</text>

< Review>
I've been a Bell Pest Control customer for years. Four months ago I moved out of state. When I called to cancel and when someone reached out to me about an upcoming service - I was told that the cancellation must be done in writing, mail a letter. In the craze of two moves in the past four months I didn't send the letter, totally spaced. So today Bell called to collect on the service that they've been providing to a vacant house. My card on file wasn't working. I informed their employee that I moved and have a local bank. I just got something in the mail from them yesterday that I hadn't opened. As we talked, I opened a bill. I reiterated that I moved in July. The employee shared that there is no way that Bell could have known that I moved if I didn't submit that information in writing. I told her that I would make the payment but it's not accurate to say that Bell didn't know that I moved. If I've told two separate employees that I moved, I've made Bell aware. Saying that the contract requires that I make the request in writing is factual - I assume. I've been a customer for years and wouldn't begin to know where to find a contract - which is why I did not contest making the payment. However, insisting that because a letter was not received, there was no way to know is not factual. And insisting to reiterate that point made for a very poor customer service experience - for no reason, I already agreed to pay. I didn't contest the payment but shared that I was annoyed and would be sure to share that dissatisfaction. Never raised my voice, didn't even change tone. And from there the service experience went further downhill fast.

The most unbelievable part of the conversation? When I shared that I would pay the $154.00 reflected on my bill today and would follow up with a the late fees at a later date and was told that I can't demand not to pay. Wait, I have to ask permission to call back to pay the late fee? Who is the customer here. Again, didn't contest it, just said I would take care of the $154 reflected on my bill today and the balance at another time (I couldn't reconcile how a bill postmarked 10/23 with no late fees has now accrued two late fees. I figured it was better to see it on a bill.). I have never experienced such terse service from Bell. Until today, everyone whom I have ever worked with has been kind. Solicitors regularly approached with competing offers. I never even entertained a conversation about switching.

I will drop a letter in the mail reflecting my cancellation as I recognize that my phone call and this note do not constitute a cancellation. Guess we could draw further that this until that until the letter is received "Bell would have no way of knowing that I've moved.". Disappointing to see my loyalty to Bell hold so little value.< /Review>

110682276381212804627< /UserId.>
< Review>
I have had Bell Pest Control Service since I purchased my first home in 2014. I recently purchased a new home in February and within the first month I had a large ant infestation in my home after an ant nest was disturbed following yard work that was done before I purchased the home. I haven't had to do any work in the yard yet, so it wasn't me:-) I called the office first thing in the morning hoping someone could come that day before the ants made it into my pantry. I wish I could remember the name of who I spoke with. She was absolutely lovely, sympathetic and went above and beyond to get techs to my house that afternoon. If I recall, she mentioned that she lives in Galt, I hope that helps her supervisor identify her.
Osmand and Isiah arrived that afternoon to spray inside and out, inspected my attic to make sure there were no rodents (as the home inspection noted some old droppings up there) and they inspected the backyard to see where the ants were coming from. Sure enough, Isiah was able to identify the source and followed the ant trail clear across my backyard to my fruit trees. They treated the area and walked me through everything they did before leaving. We set up a follow-up appointment for Osmand to return two-weeks later to check on the bait he placed in the attic and check on the ant situation.
At our follow-up appointment I informed Osmand that I thought there may be a dead rodent in my wall and I had been smelling it since the day I moved in, he also smelt it. He went straight to the attic, checked the old bait and placed an odor absorption bag in my attic to help with the odor as he couldn't find the animal. I have had Bell Pest Control Service since I purchased my first home in 2014. I recently purchased a new home in February and within the first month I had a large ant infestation in my home after an ant nest was disturbed following yard work that was done before I purchased the home. I haven't had to do any work in the yard yet, so it wasn't me:-) I called the office first thing in the morning hoping someone could come that day before the ants made it into my pantry. I wish I could remember the name of who I spoke with. She was absolutely lovely, sympathetic and went above and beyond to get techs to my house that afternoon. If I recall, she mentioned that she lives in Galt, I hope that helps her supervisor identify her.

Sure enough, Isiah was able to identify the source and followed the ant trail clear across my backyard to my fruit trees. They treated the area and walked me through everything they did before leaving. We set up a follow-up appointment for Osmand to return two-weeks later to check on the bait he placed in the attic and check on the ant situation.
